 aap ateet ke kisi bhi dalit narsanhaar kii ghatana uthaakar dekhiye
 Identity of place and caste has played a big role in the election of those who have been killed
 pichley hi saal patel aarakshan ko lekar ahmedabad main police ne kathith hinsa ke baad patel chaatro ko daudana shuru kiya
 In Ahmedabad, everyone knows that there are many societies in the area of bapunagar in which Patel resides
 un patel logon kii bhi kaaren tod di gayi jinka is pradarshan se koi lenaa-dena nahin tha

 chand pal kii deree kisi kii jaan bachaa sakati he to kisi ko maar sakati he

 baad main pataa chalata he ki kuch hindu bhi nikaale gaye jinka aaj tak pataa nahin chalaa

 agar yahi sab jaankaree computer par ek search se pal bhar main baahar jaae to sarkaar ke liye kitna aasaan hoga kisi ke kilaaf ranneeti bananaa
 It can be used for genocide and also to crush a movement
 ham aksar sunate hai ki koi vidhayak yaa saansad falaan ilaake main isliye nahin jaataa kyonki vahaan uskaa vot nahin he
 It is obvious that we, our representatives and governments have been setting our political and violent priorities based on the identity of the people and the region
 dangon ke vakt bhagalpur se lekar gujarat tak main anek kisse milenge ki hindu ko muslim ne bachaaya or muslim ko hindu ne
 If you look at the details of these anecdotes, you will find that people have fabricated many false stories about their identity
 kya aadhaar card ke baad in chand kisson ke liye koi jagah bachegi

 uske paas poochne kaa koi kaaran hi nahin hoga ki aap koun he
 She must be already knowing that you are what she is looking for
 yah sara kaam kitni tezi se or kitne bade paimaane par kiya ja sakegaa

 ham sab jaanate hai ki aam log jahaan rahete hai vahi dangon ke aasaan shikaar hote hai
 Will the information provided from Aadhaar not help the state or the government and political parties in planning riots or suppressing the police to crush any movement? The same thing happened in the Nazi era of Germany which happened against the Sikhs in Delhi
 germany main arya or yahudiyon ke nayan-naksh ke antar kaa pataa karne ke liye baqayda callipers naamak maap-yantra se jabade se lekar thobade kii napai hoti thi or is aadhaar par yahudiyon ko pakadakar gas kii bhatthi main phenk kar maar diya gaya
 This was a primitive form of biometrics and all is so common that all the information about biometrics is equipped in an organization and a computer
 aadhaar card kii sari jaankaree computer main hogi or wo bhi ek jagah
 If this search is conducted to find out where the Dalits reside in the area or where the Muslims live or where the Sikhs live or where the Hindus live, then all the information from the torso will come on the computer
 sochiye state ke haath main ye jaankaree ar suvidha he to kya ye khatara nahin he? agar yahi jaankaree rajya se hote hue privet companiyon tak pahonchegi or unke baad kis-kis tak to iske kya-kya istamaal ho sakate hai kya ham or aap thik-thik jaanate hai ? kya aap ab bhi apni pahchaan us police ke haath saunp dena chahenge jo hinsa ke vakt aapkaa kam state kaa saath zyaada detii rahi he
 The government always belongs to the government
 indian express main pratapbhanu mehta ne aadhaar card kanoon or privesi ke sawaal ko lekar ek lekh likhaa he
 If your privacy is disturbed even after this law, how will you know about it and can you go to court directly? You have to go to the same authority who is the guardian of the Aadhar card number wo praadhikaran tay karegaa ki aapke maamle ko lekar adaalat main jaaya ja saktaa he yaa nahin
 Critics are making such arguments
 sarkaar kah rahi he ki privesi ke sawaal par chintaa karne kii koi zarurat nahin he
 The Aadhaar law is quite strong
 pratapbhanu mehta ne likhaa he ki naukarshahi ko adhikaar diya gaya he ki vahi faisla karegi or usee ke hisse kaa ek doosraa samooh us faisle kii samiksha karegaa
 The Finance Minister said that privacy is not complete
 is par pratapbhanu ne likhaa he ki phir naukarshahi ko kareeb-kareeb sampurna adhikaar diye jane kaa kya tuk he
 Whenever a government reminds that privacy and freedom of expression is not final, not absolute, then the ears should be raised
 wo sarkaar zaruri nahin ki bijepi kii ho, wo congress kii bhi ho sakati he or wo telugana kii tiares kii bhi ho sakati he
 If privacy or the right to expression is not final, then where is it written that all the rights of the government are final
 sarkaar ebsolute hai
 Is it written somewhere? sarkaar bhi to ebsolute nahin he, is baat ke baavjood use hameen chunate hai or wo hamaare hone ke liye zaruri bhi he
 In support of the Aadhaar law, the US social security number has been cited, but biometric marks are not taken for the US security number like your fingers and eyes have been scanned for Aadhaar
 mishi choudhary ne bataaya he ki vahaan kaa soshal security prashasan logon ko protsaahit karata he ki pahchaan ke liye duusare vikalpon kaa istamaal karen
 In the United States, there is a Privacy Act of 1974
 is act ke tahat aam naagarik apane ricard ko dekh saktaa he
 It can request a change in it that this information is not correct or so much information can be added
 saath hi yah bhi sunishchit kiya gaya he ki aapaki jaankaree ke sandarbh main aapkaa adhikaar paribhaashit he
 It is being debated in our country whether the right to privacy is a fundamental right or not
 vaise america main bhi ye bahes hui thi
 It still happens today
